	Streams:  [][grpc](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/grpc).[StreamDesc](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/grpc#StreamDesc){},
	Metadata: "temporal/server/chasm/lib/scheduler/proto/v1/service.proto",
}

SchedulerService_ServiceDesc is the grpc.ServiceDesc for SchedulerService service. It's only intended for direct use with grpc.RegisterService, and not to be introspected or modified (even as a copy)

#### type [BackfillerState](https://github.com/temporalio/temporal/blob/v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1/message.pb.go#L275)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/server@v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1#BackfillerState "Go to BackfillerState")

type BackfillerState struct {

// Types that are valid to be assigned to Request:	//
	// *BackfillerState_BackfillRequest
	// *BackfillerState_TriggerRequest
	Request isBackfillerState_Request `protobuf_oneof:"request"`
// Every Backfiller should be assigned a unique ID upon creation, used	// for deduplication.
	BackfillId [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string) `protobuf:"bytes,6,opt,name=backfill_id,json=backfillId,proto3" json:"backfill_id,omitempty"`
// High water mark.	LastProcessedTime *[timestamppb](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/timestamppb).[Timestamp](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/timestamppb#Timestamp) `protobuf:"bytes,7,opt,name=last_processed_time,json=lastProcessedTime,proto3" json:"last_processed_time,omitempty"`
// Attempt count, incremented when the buffer is full and the Backfiller	// needs to back off before retrying to fill.
	Attempt [int64](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#int64) `protobuf:"varint,8,opt,name=attempt,proto3" json:"attempt,omitempty"`
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}

CHASM scheduler's Backfiller internal state. Backfill requests are 1:1 with Backfiller nodes. Backfiller nodes also handle immediate trigger requests.

#### type [InvokerState](https://github.com/temporalio/temporal/blob/v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1/message.pb.go#L185)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/server@v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1#InvokerState "Go to InvokerState")

type InvokerState struct {

// Buffered starts that will be started by the Invoker.	BufferedStarts []*[v11](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/server@v1.30.0/api/schedule/v1).[BufferedStart](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/server@v1.30.0/api/schedule/v1#BufferedStart) `protobuf:"bytes,2,rep,name=buffered_starts,json=bufferedStarts,proto3" json:"buffered_starts,omitempty"`
// Workflow executions that will be cancelled due to overlap policy.	CancelWorkflows []*[v12](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/common/v1).[WorkflowExecution](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/common/v1#WorkflowExecution) `protobuf:"bytes,3,rep,name=cancel_workflows,json=cancelWorkflows,proto3" json:"cancel_workflows,omitempty"`
// Workflow executions that will be terminated due to overlap policy.	TerminateWorkflows []*[v12](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/common/v1).[WorkflowExecution](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/common/v1#WorkflowExecution) `protobuf:"bytes,4,rep,name=terminate_workflows,json=terminateWorkflows,proto3" json:"terminate_workflows,omitempty"`
// High water mark, used for evaluating when to fire tasks that are backing	// off from a retry. LastProcessedTime is stored as state so that task
	// generation will be consistent, regardless of when generation occurs, such
	// as after applying a replicated state (as opposed to evaluating based on
	// present time).
	LastProcessedTime *[timestamppb](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/timestamppb).[Timestamp](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/timestamppb#Timestamp) `protobuf:"bytes,5,opt,name=last_processed_time,json=lastProcessedTime,proto3" json:"last_processed_time,omitempty"`
// A map keyed by the request ID, mapping to the workflow ID started as part	// of that request. Used to map received Nexus callbacks back to workflows.
	// Invoker adds to this mapwhen buffered starts are enqueued, and removed
	// when Invoker processes a completion.
	RequestIdToWorkflowId map[[string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)][string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string) `` /* 204-byte string literal not displayed */
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}

CHASM scheduler's Invoker internal state.

#### func (*InvokerState) [Descriptor](https://github.com/temporalio/temporal/blob/v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1/message.pb.go#L234)deprecated

type LastCompletionResult struct {
 Success *[v12](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/common/v1).[Payload](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/common/v1#Payload) `protobuf:"bytes,1,opt,name=success,proto3" json:"success,omitempty"`  Failure *[v13](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/failure/v1).[Failure](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/failure/v1#Failure) `protobuf:"bytes,2,opt,name=failure,proto3" json:"failure,omitempty"` 	// contains filtered or unexported fields

CHASM scheduler retains the payload data for the last completed workflow. Both last success and failure are stored simultaneously.

#### type [SchedulerIdleTask](https://github.com/temporalio/temporal/blob/v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1/tasks.pb.go#L28)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/server@v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1#SchedulerIdleTask "Go to SchedulerIdleTask")

type SchedulerIdleTask struct {

// Idle time total is set at time of task creation, so that if the dynamic config key	// controlling idle time changes, task validation will be aware.
	IdleTimeTotal *[durationpb](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/durationpb).[Duration](https://pkg.go.dev/google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/durationpb#Duration) `protobuf:"bytes,1,opt,name=idle_time_total,json=idleTimeTotal,proto3" json:"idle_time_total,omitempty"`
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}

Fires when the scheduler's idle period has lapsed, and the scheduler should be closed.

SchedulerServiceServer is the server API for SchedulerService service. All implementations must embed UnimplementedSchedulerServiceServer for forward compatibility

#### type [SchedulerState](https://github.com/temporalio/temporal/blob/v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1/message.pb.go#L31)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/server@v1.30.0/chasm/lib/scheduler/gen/schedulerpb/v1#SchedulerState "Go to SchedulerState")

type SchedulerState struct {

	// Scheduler request parameters and metadata.
 Schedule *[v1](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/schedule/v1).[Schedule](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/schedule/v1#Schedule) `protobuf:"bytes,2,opt,name=schedule,proto3" json:"schedule,omitempty"`  Info *[v1](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/schedule/v1).[ScheduleInfo](https://pkg.go.dev/go.temporal.io/api/schedule/v1#ScheduleInfo) `protobuf:"bytes,3,opt,name=info,proto3" json:"info,omitempty"` 	// State common to all generators is stored in the top-level machine.
 Namespace [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string) `protobuf:"bytes,5,opt,name=namespace,proto3" json:"namespace,omitempty"`  NamespaceId [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string) `protobuf:"bytes,6,opt,name=namespace_id,json=namespaceId,proto3" json:"namespace_id,omitempty"`  ScheduleId [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string) `protobuf:"bytes,7,opt,name=schedule_id,json=scheduleId,proto3" json:"schedule_id,omitempty"` // Implemented as a sequence number. Used for optimistic locking against	// update requests.
	ConflictToken [int64](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#int64) `protobuf:"varint,8,opt,name=conflict_token,json=conflictToken,proto3" json:"conflict_token,omitempty"`
// The closed flag is set true after a schedule completes, and the idle timer	// expires.
	Closed [bool](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#bool) `protobuf:"varint,9,opt,name=closed,proto3" json:"closed,omitempty"`
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}

CHASM scheduler top-level state.

type UnsafeSchedulerServiceServer interface {
	// contains filtered or unexported methods
}

UnsafeSchedulerServiceServer may be embedded to opt out of forward compatibility for this service. Use of this interface is not recommended, as added methods to SchedulerServiceServer will result in compilation errors.
